SABOO THAILAND Complete Information - English Chatbot Q&A Data
Company Basic Information
Q: What kind of company is SABOO THAILAND? A: SABOO THAILAND is a design-focused company that was the first to create fruit-shaped soaps in Thailand. Established in 2008, it's Thailand's leading natural soap manufacturing company and a global brand exporting to over 20 countries worldwide.
Q: Where are SABOO THAILAND's headquarters and stores located? A: Headquarters (Factory): 55/20 Moo 4, Tambon Bung Kham Proy, Amphur Lam Luk Ka, Pathum Thani, Thailand, 12150 SABOO THAILAND SHOP: Mixt Chatuchak, Floor 2, 8 Kamphaeng Phet 3 Rd, Chatuchak, Bangkok, Thailand, 10900 Phone: 02-159-9880, 085-595-9565 / 062-897-8962

Headquarters Phone: 02-159-9880, 085-595-9565

Q: What age groups can use these products? A: With various scents and designs tailored to different preferences, people from children to adults can purchase various product lines. Each product is manufactured considering age-appropriate safety.
Export and Business
Q: Which countries does SABOO THAILAND export to? A: We export to over 20 countries worldwide including the USA, China, Korea, Japan, Europe, Middle East, ASEAN, and Australia.
Q: Is distributorship available? A: Yes, SABOO THAILAND welcomes distributorship agreements. For details, please contact saboothailand@gmail.com or call 02-159-9880, 085-595-9565.

Fragrance and Color Safety
Q: What kind of fragrances does SABOO THAILAND use? A: We only use safe fragrances registered with IFRA (International Fragrance Association) based on European standards. All fragrances comply with international safety standards.
Q: Are there any ingredients you don't use? A: Yes, we don't use or use only within legal limits the following harmful ingredients:
Butylphenyl Methylpropional (Lilial): Banned in Europe from 2024
Hydroxycitronellal: Potential skin irritant
Cinnamal: Skin irritating ingredient
Citral: Potential allergen
Coumarin: Allergic reaction ingredient
Limonene: Potential skin irritant
Q: What kind of colorants does SABOO THAILAND use? A: We only use safe colorants used in food and high-end cosmetics. The colorants in bath products are water-soluble, so don't worry if color gets on the bathtub - it will gradually fade away.
Q: Should I worry about bathtub staining? A: No, don't worry. SABOO THAILAND products:
Use water-soluble colorants
Colors fade gradually over time even if they get on the bathtub
Use only safe colorants at food-grade level
Can be easily removed with simple cleaning after use
Q: How is fragrance safety ensured? A: - Only IFRA registered fragrances used
No harmful ingredients or use within legal limits only
Regular quality inspections and safety testing
Compliance with international cosmetic safety standards
Foam Characteristics and Surfactants
Q: What are the characteristics of SABOO THAILAND's foam? A: SABOO THAILAND's foam is special:
Chewy and long-lasting foam: Superior durability compared to regular products
Stretchy properties: Great foam for fun enjoyment
No eye irritation: So gentle it won't sting even if it gets in your eyes
Rich foam volume: Sufficient foam generation with small amounts
Q: What surfactants do you use? A: We only use EWG Grade 1 safe surfactants:
Cocamidopropyl Betaine: Coconut oil derived, EWG Grade 1
Sodium Cocoyl Isethionate: Coconut oil extracted, EWG Grade 1
Q: Why are these surfactants safe? A: - EWG Grade 1: Evaluated as the safest grade
Coconut oil derived: Extracted from natural sources
Minimized skin irritation: Low probability of causing allergies or irritation
No eye irritation: Safe with gentle ingredients
Effective cleansing power: Safe yet excellent foam and cleansing effects
Q: Is it okay if it gets in my eyes? A: Yes, SABOO THAILAND's foam is so gentle it won't sting even if it gets in your eyes. Made with EWG Grade 1 safe surfactants and natural ingredients, it's very safe.
Q: Why does the foam last so long? A: - Use of high-quality coconut-derived surfactants
Proprietary manufacturing method developed in-house
Optimal formulation perfected through 20 years of research and development
Chewy texture prevents foam from easily dissipating
Bath Bomb Usage
Q: How do I use SABOO THAILAND bubble bath bombs? A: Carbonate Type Bath Bomb: Fill the bathtub with warm water (37-40Â°C), then add the bath bomb and enjoy the process of it dissolving with a "fizzing" sound. Bubble Bar Type: Place the bubble bar under the faucet while filling with water and create foam by friction with flowing water. Bathe for about 15 minutes. Carbonate types can be finished without additional showering.
Q: Tips for creating rich foam? A: - Strong water pressure: Use strong water stream from faucet or shower head
Proper water level: Fill bathtub only 1/4 full before adding bubble bar
Friction is important: Must make direct contact with flowing water for effectiveness
Timing: Use during the water-filling process for best foam generation
Q: How do I use sebum control bath bombs? A: - Add bath bomb to warm water and let it dissolve completely
Soak your body for 15-20 minutes to let the ingredients work
Baking soda, citric acid, and natural coconut ingredients help with sebum control and pore cleansing
Recommended use 2-3 times per week
Q: What's the proper bathing time and temperature? A: - Time: About 15 minutes (maximum 20 minutes)
Temperature: 37-40Â°C (slightly higher than body temperature)
For waste elimination: 40-43Â°C
Temperature check: When your elbow feels warm in the water

Palmitic Acid: Natural fatty acid extracted from coconut/palm oil that forms skin protective barrier

Lauric Acid: Coconut oil derived ingredient with antibacterial effects and gentle cleansing power
Glycerin: 100% Thai natural glycerin with excellent moisturizing effects
Sorbitol: Natural moisturizer that maintains skin hydration

Q: What are the main ingredients in SABOO THAILAND bubble bath bombs? A: Made safely with natural ingredients:
Baking Soda: pH control, exfoliation, sebum secretion suppression, muscle relaxation
Citric Acid: Skin pH control, moisturizing and skin texture improvement, muscle relaxation with carbonic gas
Cornstarch: Relieves skin dryness, provides gentle feel
Tartaric Acid: Natural fruit acid for gentle exfoliation

Sweet Almond Oil: Rich in Vitamin E, deep moisturizing and skin soothing
Jojoba Oil: Similar structure to human sebum for quick absorption, no pore clogging

Q: What are the main ingredients in SABOO THAILAND bubble bath gel? A: Composed of safe and effective ingredients:
Sodium Cocoyl Isethionate: EWG Grade 1, coconut-derived gentle surfactant
CocoBetaine: Gentle cleansing ingredient extracted from coconut oil
Polyacrylate: Safe gelling agent for maintaining gel form
Glycerin: Forms skin moisture barrier to maintain hydration

Q: Why are these ingredients good for skin? A: Natural Fatty Acids (Palmitic, Stearic, Lauric Acid):
Similar structure to skin's natural protective barrier minimizes irritation
Provides both antibacterial and moisturizing effects simultaneously
Extracted from natural sources like coconut and palm oil
Natural Moisturizing Ingredients:
Glycerin and sorbitol attract moisture from air for long-lasting hydration
Sweet almond and jojoba oils provide deep nutrition to skin
Vitamin E helps prevent skin aging and aids regeneration
Gentle Surfactants:
All proven safe with EWG Grade 1
Coconut-derived ingredients minimize irritation
So gentle they won't sting even if they get in your eyes
Q: What are the special effects of malic acid and tartaric acid? A: - Malic Acid: Natural AHA extracted from apples that gently removes dead skin cells to improve skin tone
Tartaric Acid: Natural fruit acid derived from grapes for pore cleansing and skin texture improvement
Both are much gentler and more natural than chemical exfoliants
Safe for even sensitive skin to use
Q: Why is jojoba oil special? A: - Most similar structure to human sebum: Quick absorption, no pore clogging
Excellent oxidation stability: Doesn't deteriorate, can be stored for long periods
Suitable for all skin types: No burden even for oily skin
Deep moisturizing: Strengthens skin barrier to prevent moisture loss
Safety Guidelines
Q: What precautions should I take when using SABOO THAILAND bath bombs? A: - Proper bathing time: 15-20 minutes
Proper temperature: 37-40Â°C
Clothing caution: Avoid wearing white or easily stainable clothing
Slipping caution: Be careful as oil ingredients can make bathtub slippery
Avoid wounded or eczema areas
Check expiration date
Bathroom ventilation essential
Q: What special precautions for children? A: - Never ingest: Make sure children don't eat the products
Adult supervision required: Don't let children use alone
Storage caution: Store out of children's reach
Use small amounts: Start with less than adult portions
Made with edible ingredients but ingestion is prohibited
Q: How should sensitive skin test the products? A: If you have doubts about a product, test as follows:
Apply a small amount of powder to the weak area inside your arm
Observe for 24-48 hours
Check for allergic or skin inflammatory reactions
Use if no abnormalities, discontinue if reactions occur
Q: How to prevent slipping during bathing? A: - Oil ingredients in bath products can make bathtub slippery
Be especially careful when getting in and out of bathtub
Use of anti-slip mats recommended
Move slowly without rushing
Q: How to prevent clothes from getting stained? A: - Avoid white or easily stainable clothing
Recommend wearing bath-specific or old clothing
Change clothes immediately after bathing
Water-soluble colorants can be mostly removed by washing
Q: Can pregnant women and infants use these products? A: SABOO THAILAND products are made with edible ingredients so they're safe, but pregnant women and infants under 12 months should check product-specific precautions before use.
Q: What to do if abnormal symptoms appear? A: If red spots, swelling, itching, etc. appear, immediately stop use, rinse with running water, and consult a dermatologist if necessary.
Q: Can people with atopic dermatitis use these products? A: People with atopic dermatitis need special caution:
Must do patch test first
Start with small amounts and check reactions
Stop immediately if symptoms worsen
Recommend use after consulting with dermatologist
SABOO THAILAND is relatively safe with natural ingredients but individual differences exist

Advanced Bath Bomb Guide
Q: What's the difference between bath bombs and bubble bars? A: Bath Bomb (Carbonate Type):
Add when water is fully filled
Dissolves with "fizzing" sound spreading color and scent
Visually enjoy the dissolving process
Can finish without additional showering due to moisturizing ingredients
Bubble Bar (Foam Type):
Friction under faucet while filling water
Foam generation through interaction with flowing water
Need light shower to remove foam residue after use
Q: What are the recommended bathing time and temperature? A: - Bathing time: About 15 minutes (maximum 20 minutes)
General purpose: 37-40Â°C (slightly higher than body temperature)
For waste elimination: 40-43Â°C
Temperature check: When elbow feels warm in water
Too long bathing can strip skin moisture causing dryness
Q: How should I finish after bathing? A: Carbonate Type Bath Bomb: Just pat dry with towel without additional showering (to absorb beneficial ingredients) Bubble Bar Type: Light shower to rinse off foam residue cleanly Finishing tip: Rinsing with lukewarm or slightly cool water helps tighten open pores for skin health

Expert Advice

Q: What are expert tips for creating rich foam? A: - Water pressure is most important: Stronger water stream creates richer, chewier foam
Use shower head: Maximize foam generation by creating water flow
Proper water level: Add bubble bar after filling bathtub only 1/4 full
Additional method: Adding water forcefully with shower head or faucet creates billowing foam
Bathtub Care
Q: Will SABOO THAILAND bath bombs stain the bathtub? A: SABOO THAILAND minimizes staining issues by:
Using water-soluble colorants
Using only safe colorants at food-grade level
Mainly formulated with natural ingredients
Colors gradually fade over time
Can prevent staining by rinsing immediately after use
Q: How to remove stains if bathtub gets stained? A: Acrylic bathtub: Mix baking soda with water to make paste, use soft sponge Enamel bathtub: Use neutral detergent and baking soda, avoid strong abrasives Artificial marble bathtub: Use neutral detergent, baking soda + vinegar mixture Natural marble bathtub: Must use only pH neutral detergent, absolutely avoid acidic detergents Don't use steel wool or abrasives.
Q: How to prevent staining? A: - Rinse bathtub cleanly immediately after use
SABOO THAILAND minimizes staining risk by using water-soluble ingredients
Regular bathtub cleaning and maintenance
Rinse with water before bath bomb ingredients dry
Storage and Utilization

Store in dark places away from direct sunlight
Since they're natural ingredients, well-ventilated places are better than bathrooms
Dry completely after use before storing
Q: How can I utilize leftover bath bombs? A: - Crush into small pieces and put in cloth bags for air fresheners
Use in basins for foot baths or hand baths
Use baking soda ingredients for light cleaning (caution needed)
Small amounts can still provide sufficient effects

Problem Solving

Won't create much foam if put in already filled water
Q: My bath bomb dissolves too quickly. A: This is normal. Bath bombs are designed to immediately foam and dissolve when meeting water. Enjoy the visual effect of dissolving with "fizzing" sound.
Q: My skin feels slippery after using bath bombs. A: This is normal due to oil ingredients. Be careful when getting out of bathtub for safety, and shower lightly if needed. Use of anti-slip mats recommended.

Kerry Express Thailand Shipping Rates Guide
Q1: How much does it cost to send documents from Bangkok to Bangkok?
A: Using Envelope packaging (max 500g): 35 THB + 12 THB packaging fee = Total 47 THB
Q2: How much to send a 2kg item from Bangkok to Chiang Mai?
A: Using Mini packaging: 59 THB + 10 THB packaging fee = Total 69 THB
Q3: What's the cheapest shipping option?
A: Within Bangkok and Greater Bangkok, Envelope or Mini packaging at 35 THB is the most affordable.
Q4: How much to send a 10kg item from Bangkok to Phuket?
A: Using M packaging (max 10kg): 139 THB + 30 THB packaging fee = Total 169 THB
Q5: Why is there no packaging fee shown for XXL?
A: L, XL, and XXL sizes either don't have separate packaging fees or they're included in the shipping cost.
Q6: What's the price difference between Bangkok and other provinces?
A: Other provinces are typically 20-50 THB more expensive. For example, Mini packaging: Bangkok 35 THB vs. other zones 59 THB (24 THB difference).
Q7: What happens if the weight limit is exceeded?
A: Each packaging type has weight restrictions. If exceeded, you must choose a larger packaging size.
Q8: How long does delivery take?
A: All services offer Next Day Delivery.
Q9: What's the largest item that can be shipped?
A: XXL packaging allows up to 25kg, 200cm, costing 499 THB (for other zones).
Q10: How to send small items (under 1kg) most economically?
A: Use Envelope (500g or less) or Mini (2kg or less). Both have the same rate, so choose based on size requirements.

Contact: 1217 (Kerry Express Customer Service)
Notes:
All rates are in Thai Baht (THB)
Total cost = Shipping fee + Packaging fee
Additional terms and conditions may apply
